📝 URL and KEYWORD Format:

Add your URL and keyword into the link field with a separator. For example:
https://www.domain.com:keyword
or
http://bit.ly/xyz:keyword longtail

1 (ONE) keyword per order. To use multiple keywords create another order for the same URL using a different keyword.
5879	WorldWide Traffic from Google.com - Custom Keywords	
$0.34
500
1 000 000
📈 Tracking: Use a http://Cutt.ly link for tracking. If short url not provided, our system creates one automatically. Request this link through support tickets for delivery proof.

🔗 Link Format:

☑ Add your URL and keyword into the URL field, separated with a colon (:).
☑ Only one keyword per order.
☑ Do not include a space before/after the colon symbol. It is a single string.
☑ Keyword can be of any language, but traffic currently only comes from Google.com.

Example:
https://www.domain.com:keyword goes here

✅ Visitor Sources: Popunders, domain redirects, and our in-house traffic exchange.

✅ Start Time: Instant.
✅ Website Acceptance: All types, including adult websites.
✅ Visitor Composition: A balanced mix of desktop and mobile traffic, with an up-to-date variety of browsers and user agents.

or

1 (ONE) keyword per order. To use multiple keywords create another order for the same URL using a different keyword.
5862	Canada Traffic from Google.com Search - Custom Keywords	
$0.34
100
1 000 000
📈 Tracking: Use a http://Cutt.ly link for tracking. If short url not provided, our system creates one automatically. Request this link through support tickets for delivery proof.

🔗 Link Format:

☑ Add your URL and keyword into the URL field, separated with a colon (:).
☑ Only one keyword per order.
☑ Do not include a space before/after the colon symbol. It is a single string.
☑ Keyword can be of any language, but traffic currently only comes from Google.com.

Example:
https://www.domain.com:keyword goes here

📝 URL and KEYWORD Format:

Add your URL and keyword into the link field with a separator. For example:
https://www.domain.com:keyword
or
http://bit.ly/xyz:keyword longtail

1 (ONE) keyword per order. To use multiple keywords create another order for the same URL using a different keyword.

or
